<pictures>None</pictures>< review>
I remember building the store and getting it open in 1987, back then I called it Grand slam donuts and ice cream. Those were some great years and had great customers, from the 32oz coffee for the commuters to the baseball cards that the kids would come in to buy from the bus stop. Never had a problem with the gangs down the hill, when noon came, the less fortunate and the church‚Äôs would come by to pick up the day‚Äôs leftovers. I sold it in 89 due to a job transfer, it nice to see it has survived for so many years, I hope it remains with all the COVID stuff going on. Next time I‚Äôm in California I‚Äôll have to stop by.</review>

DISHONEST, POOR SERVICE. I went here this past Wednesday afternoon for the first time. I didn't have  cash on me, so I was happy to see the sign on the door that they accept card. I went inside and looked for any other signs that said whether or not they took card. When I asked, the woman said that they took card, but only if I bought a dozen donuts for $13. Well, I wasn't going to buy a whole dozen, so I searched my car for change and got 1 donut. The price on the glass says $1.25 each. The lady asked for $1.50. I thought, "Ok...Maybe it was a 'special' donut," and didn't make much of it. It was a pretty good raised donut with white icing and sprinkles... HOWEVER, I went back there today (Friday) in the afternoon, the same woman was there... I got two donuts of the same type- raised with icing and sprinkles- and I came prepared with a $10 bill. I gave her the $10, she muttered something like "$3.50," a little hard to hear exactly what she said, but I trusted she would charge the right amount... and she gave me $6.50 back. I didn't find out until later that she charged me $1.75 FOR EACH this time. WHATTTT??? The nerve! I hope that maybe the others who help run this business are more honest, but BEWARE. Don't let these guys cheat you on their already overpriced donuts. Take your business elsewhere if they charge you more than what they post. 4 stars for purely the yumminess of the beautiful looking donuts that I had and the fact that they're open 24 hours a day, but 3 negative stars for the lack of integrity, honesty, and friendliness from this particular woman. This business needs to get their stuff straight or they'll keep losing customers.< /text>

I joined as a member because I wanted to make sure I was engaging in a yoga practice and community 3 times a week. The teachers are lovely, skilled and elevated in their techniques. There was a large party of about 14-18 people seated next to us that was almost done when we arrived.  The rest of the restaurant was about half full.

After that it got bad.

Strike one. An Italian restaurant with no antipasto salad? Really? Ok.

Strike four. Our appetizer arrived after our food
Strike five We got bread! 3 pieces for 4 people?
Strike six. The bread was uncooked and still partially dough.

After this disaster and not eating ANYTHING I got up and took my daughter home. Luckily I drove separately.

I gave them a star for atmosphere and a star for my waitress. I'm going to assume their food is not always so horrible. One person in my party got penne arribiata, another got a Cesar salad,  and a third got Mac and cheese. I did not ask if it was good or bad but only one person commented on their food being good or bad. That was the Mac and cheese, the sauce was very thin.

I would probably try Orlando's again. Perhaps they had a new chef or something. My son has eaten their in the past and said it is very good.

< review>
One of the better TR/lead climbing gyms that I've been to. They have several autobelays set up for easy routes, which is pretty sweet for training and long ARC sessions. Smallish bouldering area that's reset very often. They offer some classes on lead climbing/multipitch/bouldering technique. Yoga is included with membership or day pass. For members they charge an initiation fee, which strikes me as a sleazy sales tactic. Minus one star for that. If they would only stop playing the same songs on repeat! Minus one star for that.< /review>

<Review>I love the stronghold! It has a relaxed atmosphere and plenty for those interested in lead or toprope climbing to do.
